// Dark background\n  const textColor = \'ffffff\'; // White text\n  const imageUrl = `https://via.placeholder.com/${width}x${height}/${backgroundColor}/${textColor}?text=${encodedName}`;\n  \n  const outputPath = path.join(imagesDir, filename);\n  \n  // Download the image\n  https.get(imageUrl, (response) => {\n    if (response.statusCode !== 200) {\n      console.error(`Failed to download image for ${name}: Status code ${response.statusCode}`);\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    const fileStream = fs.createWriteStream(outputPath);\n    response.pipe(fileStream);\n    \n    fileStream.on(\'finish\', () => {\n      fileStream.close();\n      console.log(`Generated placeholder image for ${name} at ${outputPath}`);\n    });\n  }).on(\'error\', (err) => {\n    console.error(`Error downloading image for ${name}: ${err.message}`);\n  });\n}\n\n// Generate placeholder images for each superstar\nsuperstars.forEach(superstar => {\n  generatePlaceholderImage(superstar.name, superstar.filename);\n});\n\nconsole.log(\'Started generating placeholder images. 10);\n  \n  ctx.font = \'18px Arial\';\n  ctx.fillText(\'WWE Superstar\', width / 2, height / 2 + 20);\n\n  // Save to file\n  const fileName = superstar.name.toLowerCase().replace(/\\s+/g, \'-\') + \'.jpg\';\n  const outputPath = path.join(imagesDir, fileName);\n  \n  const buffer = canvas.toBuffer(\'image/jpeg\');\n  fs.writeFileSync(outputPath, buffer);\n  console.log(`Created image for ${superstar.name} at ${outputPath}`);\n}\n\n// Create images for each superstar\nsuperstars.forEach(superstar => {\n  try {\n    createImage(superstar);\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.error(`Error creating image for ${superstar.name}: ${err.message}`);\n    \n    // Create a simple placeholder file to ensure the file exists\n    const fileName = superstar.name.toLowerCase().replace(/\\s+/g, \'-\') + \'.jpg\';\n    const outputPath = path.join(imagesDir, fileName);\n    \n    // Create an empty file\n    fs.writeFileSync(outputPath, \'\');\n    console.log(`Created empty placeholder file for ${superstar.name} at ${outputPath}`);\n  }\n});\n\nconsole.log(\'Image creation complete.\');\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

This historic merger created one of the largest publicly traded sports and entertainment companies in the world, with a combined enterprise value of over $21 billion.</p>\n                    <p>As a unified company, TKO leverages the global reach, passionate fan bases, and complementary content offerings of both WWE and UFC to maximize value for shareholders, partners, and the millions of fans around the world.   <h2 class="section-title">World Championships</h2>\n            \n            <!-- WWE Championship -->\n            <div class="championship-detail" id="wwe-championship">\n                <div class="championship-image">\n                    <img src="https://www.wwe.com/f/styles/wwe_16_9_l/public/all/2023/04/WWE_Championship_Cody_Rhodes--a9d9e6a6b3c6d5a7e2d1e0b8b3c4d9e8.png" alt="WWE Championship">\n                    <div class="championship-image-overlay">\n                        <h3>Established: 1963</h3>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="championship-info">\n                    <h2 class="championship-name">WWE Championship</h2>\n                    <div class="championship-holder">\n                        <img src="../assets/images/superstars/cody-rhodes.jpg" alt="Cody Rhodes" class="holder-image">\n                        <div class="holder-info">\n                            <h3>Cody Rhodes</h3>\n                            <p class="reign-info">50+ days • 2nd reign</p>\n                            <p>Won at SummerSlam 2025 (August 3, 2025)</p>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                    <p>The WWE Championship is the most prestigious title in WWE and one of the most coveted championships in professional wrestling history. It represents the pinnacle of achievement in WWE and is contested exclusively on the SmackDown brand.</p>\n                    <p>The current design features a large WWE logo in the center with customizable side plates for each champion. The championship has been held by legends such as Bruno Sammartino, Hulk Hogan, "Stone Cold" Steve Austin, The Rock, John Cena, and Roman Reigns.</p>\n                    \n                    <div class="championship-history">\n                        <h3 class="history-title">Recent Champions</h3>\n                        <div class="previous-holders">\n                            <div                </div>\n                            <div class="previous-holder">\n                                <img src="../assets/images/superstars/cody-rhodes.jpg" alt="Cody Rhodes">\n                                <p>Cody Rhodes</p>\n                            </div>\n                            <div class="previous-holder">\n                                <img src="../assets/images/superstars/roman-reigns.jpg" alt="Roman Reigns">\n                                <p>Roman Reigns</p>\n                            </div>\n                            <div         <p>Big E</p>\n                            </div>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    <div class="notable-champions">\n                        <h3 class="history-title">Notable Champions</h3>\n                        <ul>\n                            <li><strong>Bruno Sammartino:</strong> Longest reign (2,803 days)</li>\n                            <li><strong>John Cena:</strong> Most reigns (13)</li>\n                            <li><strong>Hulk Hogan:</strong> Defined the 1980s "Rock \'n\' Wrestling" era</li>\n                            <li><strong>Stone Cold Steve Austin:</strong> Face of the Attitude Era</li>\n                            <li><strong>The Rock:</strong> "The People\'s Champion"</li>\n                            <li><strong>Roman Reigns:</strong> Modern era record holder (1,316 days)</li>\n                            <li><strong>Brock Lesnar:</strong> Dominant force of the modern era</li>\n                            <li><strong>Randy Orton:</strong> "The Legend Killer" with 10 reigns</li>\n                        </ul>\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    <div class="championship-facts">\n                        <h4>Championship Facts</h4>\n                        <ul>\n                            <li>Originally known as the WWWF World Heavyweight Championship</li>\n                            <li>Has been unified with other world titles multiple times</li>\n                            <li>Current design introduced in 2013, with minor updates since</li>\n                            <li>Has been defended in 30+ countries worldwide</li>\n                            <li>Main evented WrestleMania 39 times</li>\n                        </ul>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n            \n            <!-- World Heavyweight Championship -->\n            <div class="championship-detail" id="world-heavyweight-championship">\n                <div class="championship-image">\n                    <img src="https://www.wwe.com/f/styles/wwe_16_9_l/public/all/2023/05/20230527_KOTR_Seth_WHC--a9d9e6a6b3c6d5a7e2d1e0b8b3c4d9e8.jpg" alt="World Heavyweight Championship">\n                    <div class="championship-image-overlay">\n                        <h3>Established: 2023 (Current version)</h3>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="championship-info">\n                    <h2 class="championship-name">World Heavyweight Championship</h2>\n                    <div class="championship-holder">\n                        <img src="../assets/images/superstars/seth-rollins.jpg" alt="Seth Rollins" class="holder-image">\n                        <div class="holder-info">\n                            <h3>Seth Rollins</h3>\n                            <p class="reign-info">75+ days • 3rd reign</p>\n                            <p>Won at Money in the Bank 2025 (July 6, 2025)</p>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                    <p>The World Heavyweight Championship was reintroduced in 2023 as Raw\'s premier championship after the WWE Championship became exclusive to SmackDown. It represents the highest achievement for superstars on the Raw brand.</p>\n                    <p>The current design features a large center plate with a globe design and the WWE logo prominently displayed. The championship pays homage to the legacy of world championships in wrestling while establishing its own prestigious lineage.</p>\n                    \n                    <div class="championship-history">\n                        <h3 class="history-title">Recent Champions</h3>\n                        <div class="previous-holders">\n                            <div            </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- Women\'s Championships -->\n        <div class="championship-content" data-id="womens">\n            <h2 <div class="championship-image">\n                    <img src="https://www.wwe.com/f/styles/wwe_16_9_l/public/all/2023/05/20230527_KOTR_Asuka_WWE_Womens--a9d9e6a6b3c6d5a7e2d1e0b8b3c4d9e8.jpg" brand. It represents the highest achievement for female superstars on SmackDown and continues the legacy of women\'s wrestling in WWE.</p>\n                    <p>The current design features a white strap with gold plates, prominently displaying the WWE logo. The championship was introduced in 2023 as part of WWE\'s brand split championship structure.</p>\n                    \n                    <div class="championship-history">\n            </div>\n            \n            <!-- Women\'s World Championship -->\n            <div class="championship-detail" id="womens-world-championship">\n                <div class="championship-image">\n                    <img src="https://www.wwe.com/f/styles/wwe_16_9_l/public/all/2023/05/20230527_KOTR_Belair_Womens_World--a9d9e6a6b3c6d5a7e2d1e0b8b3c4d9e8.jpg"      </div>\n                    </div>\n                    <p>The Women\'s World Championship is the premier women\'s title on the Raw brand. It represents the highest achievement for female superstars on Raw and was created to mirror the World Heavyweight Championship structure.</p>\n                    <p>The current design features a red strap with gold plates, prominently displaying a globe design similar to the World Heavyweight Championship. The championship was introduced in 2023 as part of WWE\'s brand split championship structure.</p>\n                    \n                    <div class="championship-history">\n       <!-- Women\'s Intercontinental Championship -->\n            <div class="championship-detail" id="womens-intercontinental-championship">\n                <div class="championship-image">\n                          <p class="reign-info">150+ days • 1st reign</p>\n                            <p>Won at WrestleMania 41 (April 19, 2025)</p>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                    <p>The Women\'s Intercontinental Championship was introduced in 2024 as a midcard championship for the women\'s division on Raw. It provides another avenue for female superstars to showcase their talents and elevate their careers.</p>\n                    <p>The design is inspired by the men\'s Intercontinental Championship but features unique elements that distinguish it as a premier women\'s title. The white strap with gold and blue accents gives it a distinctive look.</p>\n                    \n                    <div class="championship-history">\n                        <h3 class="history-title">All Champions</h3>\n                        <div class="previous-holders">\n                            <div class="previous-holder">\n                                <img               <li><strong>Becky Lynch:</strong> Longest-reigning champion (150+ days and counting)</li>\n                        </ul>\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    <div class="championship-facts">\n                        <h4>Championship Facts</h4>\n                        <ul>\n                            <li>Created in 2024 to provide more championship class="championship-content" data-id="midcard">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Midcard Championships</h2>\n            \n            <!-- Intercontinental Championship -->\n            <div class="championship-detail" id="intercontinental-championship">\n                <div class="championship-image">\n                    <img src="https://www.wwe.com/f/styles/wwe_16_9_l/public/all/2019/05/20190520_RAW_Miz_24_7--a9d9e6a6b3c6d5a7e2d1e0b8b3c4d9e8.jpg" alt="Intercontinental Championship">\n                    <div class="championship-image-overlay">\n                        <h3>Established: 1979</h3>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="championship-info">\n                    <h2 class="championship-name">Intercontinental Championship</h2>\n                    <div class="championship-holder">\n                        <img src="../assets/images/superstars/jey-uso.jpg" alt="Jey Uso" class="holder-image">\n                        <div class="holder-info">\n                            <h3>Jey Uso</h3>\n                            <p class="reign-info">30+ days • 1st reign</p>\n                            <p>Won at SummerSlam 2025 (August 3, 2025)</p>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                    <p>The Intercontinental Championship is one of WWE\'s most prestigious midcard titles and has been held by some of the greatest technical wrestlers in history. Often referred to as the "workhorse championship," it represents excellence in in-ring performance.</p>\n                    <p>The current design is a modernized version of the classic white-strapped Intercontinental Championship, featuring a white leather strap with a centerpiece displaying a globe and continental design elements.</p>\n                    \n                    <div class="championship-history">\n                        <h3 class="history-title">Recent Champions</h3>\n                        <div class="previous-holders">\n                            <div class="previous-holder">\n                                <img src="../assets/images/superstars/gunther.jpg" alt="Gunther">\n                                <p>Gunther</p>\n                            </div>\n                            <div class="previous-holder">\n                                <img src="../assets/images/superstars/sami-zayn.jpg" alt="Sami Zayn">\n                                <p>Sami Zayn</p>\n                            </div>\n                            <div class="previous-holder">\n                                <img src="../assets/images/superstars/dominik-mysterio.jpg" alt="Dominik Mysterio">\n                                <p>Dominik Mysterio</p>\n                            </div>\n      </div>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    <div class="notable-champions">\n                        <h3 class="history-title">Notable Champions</h3>\n                        <ul>\n                            <li><strong>Gunther:</strong> Longest reign (666 days)</li>\n                            <li><strong>The Honky Tonk Man:</strong> Longest reign of classic era (454 days)</li>\n                            <li><strong>Chris Jericho:</strong> Most reigns (9)</li>\n                            <li><strong>Pat Patterson:</strong> First champion</li>\n                            <li><strong>Randy Savage:</strong> Iconic match with Ricky Steamboat at WrestleMania III</li>\n                            <li><strong>Shawn Michaels:</strong> Legendary ladder match with Razor Ramon</li>\n                            <li><strong>The Rock:</strong> First championship in WWE</li>\n                            <li><strong>Razor Ramon:</strong> Defined the championship in the 1990s</li>\n                        </ul>\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    <div class="championship-facts">\n                        <h4>Championship Facts</h4>\n                        <ul>\n                            <li>Created in 1979 as a championship for wrestlers from different continents</li>\n                            <li>Has been held by over 80 different champions</li>\n                            <li>Often considered a stepping stone to world championship status</li>\n                            <li>Has featured in some of the most iconic matches in WWE history</li>\n                            <li>Current design is a modernized version of the classic "white strap" look</li>\n                        </ul>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n            \n            <!-- United States Championship -->\n            <div class="championship-detail" id="united-states-championship">\n                <div class="championship-image">\n                    <img src="https://www.wwe.com/f/styles/wwe_16_9_l/public/all/2020/01/20200127_RAW_AndradeDQ_HP--a9d9e6a6b3c6d5a7e2d1e0b8b3c4d9e8.jpg" alt="United States Championship">\n                    <div class="championship-image-overlay">\n                        <h3>Established: 1975 (WWE version since 2001)</h3>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="championship-info">\n                    <h2 class="championship-name">United States Championship</h2>\n                    <div class="championship-holder">\n                        <img src="../assets/images/superstars/sami-zayn.jpg" alt="Sami Zayn" class="holder-image">\n                        <div class="holder-info">\n                            <h3>Sami Zayn</h3>\n                            <p class="reign-info">90+ days • 3rd reign</p>\n                            <p>Won at Clash at the Castle 2025 (May 25, 2025)</p>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                    <p>The United States Championship has a rich history dating back to 1975 in the NWA/WCW before being incorporated into WWE in 2001. with red, white, and blue accents on a black leather strap, prominently displaying the United States eagle and shield.</p>\n                    \n                    <div
